msg:Zhaolong Hotel. It was originally the first five-star hotel built with donations from the Bao family introduced by Deng Xiaoping in the 1980s during Beijing's reform and opening up. I stayed there seven or eight years ago. Although the facilities are a bit old. But the style of the old five-star hotel is still there. This trip has been taken over by the First Brigade. When I entered the store, I was surprised. The original five-star hotel has been transformed into a convenience hotel. The lobby is gone too. Check-in procedures are done at the two workstations on the second floor. When I checked in, the filter criteria was to select five stars. After I checked in, I took a closer look and found that it was five diamonds. This is a routine of Ctrip. Stars are stars. If you want diamonds, you should be diamonds. Confuse diamonds with stars. Ctrip really has you.
Because I do it out of trust. It must be a week online. Searched last week, the price is 1,400 yuan per room per day for check-in from September 5 to check-out on September 10 (see Figure 1). I originally thought that a five-star hotel should cost this price, so I booked and paid without hesitation. When I arrived and saw the hotel like this, I felt very disappointed. Checking the hotel price again, it has been reduced to 1,283 yuan/room per day. So I complained to Ctrip. The girl from Ctrip was very nice. She immediately helped me cancel my stay for the next 4 days and then check in for another 4 days (see Figure 4). She also explained to me that the prices for two of the weekends should be more expensive, which I accepted. . When I arrived on Friday, I took another look at the price on Ctrip. The price actually dropped to 1,143 yuan/room per day on the weekend. Oh my gosh, I must have been a little too big. No wonder Ctrip rated me as a Golden Diamond member. What exactly is the problem with Ctrip? Is it because I am a leek?
